< Text>
I love Black Market Meal Prep! I've been coming here for years since they've been open. I can't believe it's taken me so long to actually post a review. The customer service and energy that they have here is stellar and infectious. Luis in particular is amazing and and an absolute rockstar. He's attentive and you get the feeling that he genuinely cares about his team and clients. He's always greeting people by name and with a smile that finds its way through the face mask. The entire team has great customer service.

The food is also delicious! I was craving healthy and tasty food options after workouts years ago when I came across Black Market Meal Prep online. My first dine in meal was a chicken build your own entree and I was hooked. I was so excited that I couldn't stop recommending the place to anyone that would listen from my gym, work, and friends. It's been who knows how years and I still have that same enthusiasm. I've gotten my new co-workers hooked on their meals and the protein donuts they distribute. I'd highly recommend trying their restaurant and meal prep service. Bison burger and chicken anything for the dine in are my go tos. I'm partial to their chicken and beef options for the meal prep. I tend to stay away from the fish meals. Philippino chicken, kbbq beef, and   ¬øMexican market?, I think it's called, style chicken are my favorite meal preps.

Keep up the awesome work</Text>

Craig Wilson<//username>
< Text>
We've had to spend quite a bit of time at St Joseph Hospital due to a family member being there and today we wanted to venture out to find some food other than Hospital cafeteria food. We were going to go into Togo's but I noticed the sign on the door and immediately thought it was a place to go in make dinners that you would take home to eat later. Turns out it's a nice little restaurant making some seriously good food. Nothing complicated here you pick a protein which can range from chicken to veggie patty to fish. You then pick a vegetable and last you pick a carb which can range from sweet potatoes to rice. I ordered a beverage and they have the natural sodas dispensed in a fountain that were very good. They provide alkaline water that's chilled for free. We sat down in a booth that was clean and the silverware was nicely wrapped in a paper napkin. We waited about 10 minutes for our food. We were pleasantly surprised to have a very simple meal that tasted excellent. We both had the chicken which was tender, seasoned and grilled nicely. I had three vegetables and no carbs. The vegetables were cooked perfect meaning not overdone or too crunchy and nicely seasoned. I honestly could eat here everyday substituting my chicken for fish. The owner was in and we talked for a few minutes, nice guy. This is a terrific find and we'll definitely be back soon.</Text>

< Text>
Not at all surprised this place has such a good rating.

I didn't check reviews or anything, just wanted to stop by a local gun store and ask some questions about guns (total newbie btw, literally never shot a gun in my life).

The small store is absolutely packed with fishing gear n stuff, but I was able to see down the short hallway to a counter with some handguns and shotguns on display

Once I got back there I was greeted warmly and I began perusing the selection and asking my questions.

Not once did I feel any embarrassment or awkwardness or anything. I'm sure he answered many of my questions a million times but he delivered consistently great customer service.

If you're a first timer you'll need an fsc to buy a gun. They do it there for 25 bucks. I'd highly recommend choosing this place, since he was so beginner friendly.< /Text>

<rate>5< /rate>< review>
Always great. I've made purchases here regularly here for over 11 years. Just making an observation of a comment from a customer who purchased a used SKS. A firearm was purchased and the serial number is registered to you; it becomes a matter of factory service or warranty. You cannot just swap out a firearm with another as you would a TV at Best Buy; there is red tape and govt paperwork that is registered to the firearm in question. Think before you buy or whine about that purchase.<//review>

The staff was quite friendly, and the outdoor seating is beautiful. The menu is a bit pricey, and the quality of the meal itself was decent once, and just okay another time. My wife enjoyed the egg white omelet for breakfast one morning, which was solid, while I had the eggs Benedict which was exactly as advertised. We went back for lunch the next day (because let‚Äôs be honest, the hotel has limited food options) and we were both disappointed in our respective choices of a chicken panini and the lamb burger (I‚Äôm a fan of blue cheese, but damn!).
The primary reason for my 2-star assessment is that the service was unjustifiably slow for both meals. We sat for breakfast at 10:00 on a Friday and waited 10 minutes for coffee, and an additional 30 for our fairly basic egg dishes. We sat at 11:00 on Saturday when the restaurant was at ~30%, were sat without menus, ordered about 15 minutes later, and didn‚Äôt have meals in front of us until 11:40. We later realized that we also never received the Diet Coke my wife ordered.
Today, we went to the coffee shop and got bagels for breakfast. I‚Äôd rather eat at the airport than try my luck at pinzimini for a third time. The other 6 reviews look good, so maybe they are just having an off weekend, but I won‚Äôt be back to find out.<//text>
